            $('.mb-gutter .property-card').each(function(){

                $(this).find('a').on('click', function(){
    
                    setTimeout(function() { 
                        var host = window.location.origin;
                        var urlparam = window.location.pathname;
                        window.location = host + urlparam;
                        console.log('init');
                    }, 2000);
                });
            });


			if($('.page-template-page--contact')[0]){
				var refresh = window.localStorage.getItem('refresh');
				if (refresh===null){
					window.location.reload();
					window.localStorage.setItem('refresh', "1");
				}

                $('.location-maps__location a.font-medium').each(function(){
                    
                    $(this).on('click', function(e){
                        e.preventDefault();
                        var a = $(this).attr('href');
                        window.open(a, '_blank');
                    });
                });
			}

            
            $('nav.main-menu-right li').eq(3).find('a').on('click', function(){
                var a = $(this).attr('href');
                window.open(a, '_self');
            });

    <script>
        jQuery(document).ready(function($){
            if($('.page-id-9')[0]){
                // Make an AJAX request to the API
                rentalAPIURL = '/wp-json/rentals/v1/current';
                $.ajax({
                    url: rentalAPIURL,
                    type: 'GET',
                    success: function(data) {
                        // Handle successful API response
                        $.each(data, function(index, rental){
                            // Do something with each element/rental
                            $('h2:contains("Rentals")').next('ul').append('<li><a href="'+rental.link+'">'+rental.title+'</a></li>');
                        });
                    },
                    error: function(error) {
                        // Handle error
                        console.error('Error fetching data:', error);
                    }
                });

            }

        });
    </script>

    <script>
        jQuery(document).ready(function($){
            if($('.page-template-page--property-map')[0]){
                var path = window.location.pathname;
                var a = path.replace(/\//g, '');

                if(a == 'sold'){
                    $('.page-template-page--property-map .single-property-footer-link').attr('href', 'https://www.homely.com.au/real-estate-agency/pulse-property-group-30968/sold-properties');
                }
                if(a == 'rent'){
                    $('.page-template-page--property-map .single-property-footer-link').attr('href', 'https://www.homely.com.au/real-estate-agency/pulse-property-group-30968/properties-for-rent');
                }
                if(a == 'buy'){
                    $('.page-template-page--property-map .single-property-footer-link').attr('href', 'https://www.homely.com.au/real-estate-agency/pulse-property-group-30968/properties-for-sale');
                }
            }
        });
    </script>
